CHENNAI, THURSDAY, SEPTEMBER 8, 2011

MUNICIPAL ADMINISTRATION AND WATER SUPPLY DEPARTMENT
PROPASAL FOR DELIMITATION OF THE MUNICIPAL COUNCILS OF CERTAIN DISTRICTS UNDER THE
TAMIL NADU DISTRICT MUNICIPALITIES ACT.
TIRUPATHUR MUNICIPALITY
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 125, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™ («î˜î™)¶¬ø, 8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011]
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(F-1)/2011.
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of section 43 of the Tamil Nadu District Municipalities
Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession of all previous notifications issued on the subject,
the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consulting the municipal council of Tirupathur municipality, hereby divides
the Tirupathur municipality into thirty six territorial wards for the purpose of election of thirty six councillors  and
hereby fixes  the boundaries of the said thirty six wards as described in the Schedule below:—
2.  This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the municipal council of Tirupathur
municipality.
DTP—II-2 Ex. (317)—1

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
13
KANCHEEPURAM  MUNICIPALITY 
 [Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 126, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø, 8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011] 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-2)/2011. 
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of section 43 of the                 
Tamil Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession 
of all previous notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after 
consulting the Municipal council of the Kancheepuram Municipality, hereby divides the 
Kancheepuram Municipality into fifty one territorial wards for the purpose of election of fifty 
one councillors and  hereby fixes the boundaries of the said fifty one wards as described in 
the Schedule below:-- 
          2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the Municipal 
Council of Kancheepuram Municipality.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
26 
HOSUR  MUNICIPALITY 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡. 127, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011.] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-3)/2011. 
 
 
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of Section 43 of the  
Tamil Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession 
of all previous notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu after consulting 
the Municipal council of the Hosur Municipality, hereby divides the Hosur Municipality into forty 
five territorial wards for the purpose of election of forty five councillors and hereby fixes the 
boundaries of the said forty five wards as described in the schedule below:-- 
 
 
2.  This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary election to the Municipal 
council of Hosur Municipality.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
 
38 
KARUR  MUNICIPALITY 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 128, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø, 8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011.] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-4)/2011. 
 
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of Section 43  of the 
Tamil Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in 
supersession of all previous notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil 
Nadu, after consulting the municipal council of Karur Municipality, hereby  divides the  
Karur Municipality into forty eight territorial wards for the purpose of election of forty 
eight  councillors and  hereby fixes the boundaries of the said forty eight wards as 
described in the Schedule below:--- 
 
2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the 
council of municipal council of Karur Municipality. 
 
THE SCHEDULE 
 
 
Ward 
No. 
Boundaries                             
(North West - Clock Wise) 
Existing 
Local Body 
Existing 
Ward 
No. 
Assembly 
Constituency

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
 
51
NAGERCOIL  MUNICIPALITY 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 129, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-5)/2011. 
 
 
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of Section 43 of the Tamil 
Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession of all 
previous  notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consulting the 
Municipal Council of Nagercoil Municipality, hereby divides the Nagercoil Municipality into 
fifty two territorial wards for the purpose of election of fifty two councillors and hereby fixes 
the boundaries of the said fifty two wards as described in the Schedule below:-- 
 
            2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the Municipal 
council of Nagercoil Municipality.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
 
 
69
NAMAKKAL  MUNICIPALITY 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 130, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011.] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-6)/2011. 
 
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of section 43 of the Tamil Nadu 
District Municipalities Act, 1920 ( Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession of all previous 
notifications issued on the  subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consulting the municipal 
council of Namakkal municipality, hereby  divides the  Namakkal Municipality  into thirty nine 
territorial wards for the purpose of election of thirty nine councillors  and hereby fixes  the 
boundaries of the said thirty nine wards as described in the Schedule below:--            
2.This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the municipal 
council of Namakkal \Municipality.  
THE SCHEDULE.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
 
84
VILLUPURAM  MUNICIPALITY 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 131, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011] 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-7)/2011. 
         In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of Section 43 of the Tamil Nadu 
District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession of all previous 
Notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consulting the municipal 
council of the Villupuram Municipality, hereby divides the Villupuram Municipality into forty two 
territorial wards for the purpose of election of forty two councillors and hereby fixes  the 
boundaries of the said forty two wards as described in the Schedule below:--- 
              2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the municipal 
council of Villupuram Municipality.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
92 
PUDUKKOTTAI  MUNICIPALITY 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 132, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™  
(«î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  8 ªêŠì‹ð˜ 2011] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/396(f-8)/2011. 
 
                                                        
 
            In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of section 43 of the 
Tamil Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and in supersession 
of all previous notifications issued on the subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after 
consulting the Municipal council of the Pudukkottai Municipality, hereby divides the 
Pudukkottai municipality into forty two territorial wards for the purpose of election of forty two 
councilors  and hereby fixes  the boundaries of the said forty two wards as described in the 
schedule below:-- 
              2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the Municipal 
council of Pudukkottai Municipality.
